<div id="review_167093213" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/167093213" />
    <a title="Stephanie (Stepping Out Of The Page)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2485722-stephanie-stepping-out-of-the-page"><img alt="Stephanie (Stepping Out Of The Page)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1579948413p2/2485722.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/167093213?book_show_action=true">May 10, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stephanie (Stepping Out Of The Page)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stephanie (Stepping Out Of The Page)" href="/user/show/2485722-stephanie-stepping-out-of-the-page">Stephanie (Stepping Out Of The Page)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781419700477" href="/book/show/10806009-the-storyteller">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2485722-stephanie-stepping-out-of-the-page?shelf=arc-or-review">arc-or-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2485722-stephanie-stepping-out-of-the-page?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2485722-stephanie-stepping-out-of-the-page?shelf=realistic-fiction">realistic-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2485722-stephanie-stepping-out-of-the-page?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2485722-stephanie-stepping-out-of-the-page?shelf=crime-thriller-mystery">crime-thriller-mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2485722-stephanie-stepping-out-of-the-page?shelf=really-good">really-good</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2485722-stephanie-stepping-out-of-the-page?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2485722-stephanie-stepping-out-of-the-page?shelf=cover-appeal">cover-appeal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2485722-stephanie-stepping-out-of-the-page?shelf=rape">rape</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2485722-stephanie-stepping-out-of-the-page?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer167093213" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9068778263350408657">This is a book that completely and utterly blew me away! I admit that I was a little daunted by it at first. The premise sounded good, but I was slightly unsure about the fairy tale element of it - a lot of the time, this just doesn't work for me. This also book is reasonably thick with small font, and I always have to finish books that I start, so I really, really hoped that this was good. The Storyteller wasn't good though, it was amazing. I don't know if much was lost in translation from Germ</span>
  <span id="freeText9068778263350408657" style="display:none">This is a book that completely and utterly blew me away! I admit that I was a little daunted by it at first. The premise sounded good, but I was slightly unsure about the fairy tale element of it - a lot of the time, this just doesn't work for me. This also book is reasonably thick with small font, and I always have to finish books that I start, so I really, really hoped that this was good. The Storyteller wasn't good though, it was amazing. I don't know if much was lost in translation from German to English, but the result was still beautiful.<br /><br />This book seems to have a little something for everyone. I'd class it as Young Adult, but it is bordering on being adult fiction. There is a contemporary, somewhat coming of age aspect to this book. There are mysteries, at points it becomes a thriller with crimes that we are wanting to solve. There is a fantasy aspect, as The Storyteller tells us a fairy tale - but it's also very much real, the events in the story reflecting real-life. The fairytale is a form of escapism against the harsh reality and a form of communication between our three main characters.<br /><br />This is a very vivid and dark novel. I wouldn't say that it's sinister as such, but there is something about it that is haunting and disturbing. It deals with a whole lot of very difficult subjects. The setting feels stark, cold and true to life. The pace is quite relaxed from the beginning until the last quarter of the book, where things really speed up. Although the pace was relaxed, I never became bored. Reading about both the fairy tale world and the real world was equally fascinating. There was always something that I wanted to know more about, especially when we were given not one, but two murder mysteries.<br /><br />We are introduced to a lot of different characters in this story but, thankfully, it doesn't become confusing. Every character plays an important part and have strong foundations. Our main characters are Anna, a girl from a well-to-do family and an intriguing boy whom she meets at her school, Abel, who lives with his young sister, Micha, in a prison-like tower block. All three of these characters are unbelievably complex and watching their relationships develop and change is very interesting. Their worlds are very different, but seeing how they work together and the contrast of their lives has a very strong effect. Anna and Abel's relationship was hesitant but natural. They certainly worked well together and the chemistry was there. <br /><br />Abel does everything he can to protect his little sister, Micha - he is more of a father figure to her. This protectiveness is admirable and understandable. It really made me warm to Abel, despite some uncertainty that I did have about him. He is such a well developed character and I really did sympathise with him. At points I adored him and at points I simply hated his choices. There is a lot of different layers to him and towards the end, when I was discovering more and more about him, it actually became a little painful. It was heart and gut wrenching. During the last quarter of the book, my emotions were thrown around a lot, with Michaelis revealing so many secrets and some of the answers to questions that were in the back of my mind from the start. I can imagine that a lot of people will be displeased with what happens nearing the end as it is shocking and very raw - the author doesn't hold anything back.<br /><br />There is a lot more to this book than I can mention in a review, especially without including spoilers. I would recommend this to anyone who is aged 16+ who feels as though they could deal with some dark issues and that want a thrilling, enthralling read. Prepare to have your emotions tested and to have story stay with you for a long time after finishing it. I wouldn't hesitate to pick up another book by Michaelis, this was very different and truly fantastic. A book that certainly makes an impact.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9068778263350408657" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('IPMt5vXfdwKmug6W1KEz4J+B1mTcFegAp7FJNOJEprEbwrBQoSKftp6y2WXi+a3qb1LLd5NPvVrs+bG09cUr1w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ulZA1P53aw27BXPIaVxbbP55/eQNiXzSux7pyX8kU6SBZ91iqoqDuYMNpDtfBMVmDqrg90LTKYjwVhFJaKXewg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/14863867-der-m-rchenerz-hler">Quotes from The Storyteller</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;Just a tiny little pain,<br />Three days of heavy rain,<br />Three days of sunlight,<br />Everything will be alright,<br />Just a tiny little pain.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/510595-just-a-tiny-little-pain-three-days-of-heavy-rain">225 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;My child, I know you're not a child<br />But I still see you running wild<br />Between those flowering trees.<br />Your sparkling dreams, your silver laugh<br />Your wishes to the stars above <br />Are just my memories.<br /><br />And in your eyes the ocean<br />And in your eyes the sea<br />The waters frozen over<br />With your longing to be free.<br /><br />Yesterday you'd awoken<br />To a world incredibly old.<br />This is the age you are broken<br />Or turned into gold.<br /><br />You had to kill this child, I know.<br />To break the arrows and the bow<br />To shed your skin and change.<br />The trees are flowering no more<br />There's blood upon the tiles floor<br />This place is dark and strange.<br /><br />I see you standing in the storm<br />Holding the curse of youth<br />Each of you with your story<br />Each of you with your truth.<br /><br />Some words will never be spoken<br />Some stories will never be told.<br />This is the age you are broken<br />Or turned into gold.<br /><br />I didn't say the world was good.<br />I hoped by now you understood<br />Why I could never lie.<br />I didn't promise you a thing. <br />Don't ask my wintervoice for spring<br />Just spread your wings and fly.<br /><br />Though in the hidden garden<br />Down by the green green lane<br />The plant of love grows next to<br />The tree of hate and pain.<br /><br />So take my tears as a token.<br />They'll keep you warm in the cold.<br />This is the age you are broken<br />Or turned into gold.<br /><br />You've lived too long among us<br />To leave without a trace<br />You've lived too short to understand<br />A thing about this place.<br /><br />Some of you just sit there smoking<br />And some are already sold. <br />This is the age you are broken<br />Or turned into gold.<br />This is the age you are broken or turned into gold.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/575567-my-child-i-know-you-re-not-a-child-but-i">216 likes</a>
            </nobr>
